                                    Summary
Fourteen weIls and one canal were sampIed at the Friesian Farms Dairy by DeGroot Environmental personnel.
SampIes were coIlected on JuIy 10, and September 20, 2023. The sampIes coIlected are listed beIow.
EIectrical conductivity (EC) was measured in the laboratory. Ammonium presence was measured in the fieId
using test strips. ResuIts were recorded on the sampIing record for each sampIe coIlected. SampIes were
coIlected in bottIes provided by the testing laboratory. The sampies were pIaced in a cooIer with ice packs and
deIivered to BSK AnaIytical Laboratories, an ELAP laboratory. WeIl sampIes were anaIyzed as defined in the
MRP, updated in February 2011. The five year anaIysis was performed on approximateIy 20 of the weIls
sampIed. ,

Friesian Farms
Groundwater Monitoring Report 2023
Il. INTRODUCTION
The foIlowing is the 2023 Groundwater Monitoring Report for the Friesian Farms
Dairy faciIity located at 5593 Avenue 176, TuIare, TuIare County, CaIifornia
(Site). The Site is located west of Road 56, and south of Avenue 176,
approximateIy five and one-haIf miIes east of the City of Corcoran. The dairy site
is within Sections 10 and 14, Township 21 South, Range 23 East, Mount DiabIo
BaseIine and Meridian.
ll. GROUNDWATER SAMPLING AND MEASUREMENT DATA
A. Monitoring WeIl SampIing Procedures
Provost & Pritchard ConsuIting Group (Provost & Pritchard) personnel
attempted to sampIe groundwater monitoring weIls MW-1 through MW-3 on
March 08 and September 06, 2023. Monitoring weIl MW-1 through MW-3
were dry during the March 08, 2023, sampIing event. Monitoring weIls MW-1
and MW-3 were dry during the September 06, 2023, sampIing event.
Monitoring weIl MW-2 had sufficient water to aIlow for sampIing.
When sufficient groundwater is avaiIabIe for sampIing or measurement, static
water level is measured from the top of each PVC casing and recorded to the
nearest 0.01 foot with respect to the estabIished casing eIevation, as
possibIe. Each sampIed monitoring weIl is purged a minimum of three weIl
voIumes, as possibIe. Purged water is monitored for pH, eIectrical
conductivity (EC), and temperature.
Each monitoring weIl is equipped with a dedicated Waterra inertia pump and
Waterra tubing. The use of dedicated sampIing equipment prevents cross-
contamination between sampIes and eIiminates the need for fieId
decontamination of the equipment. SampIe containers are steriIized and
transported to the fieId under conditions to preserve their steriIity.
Groundwater sampIes coIlected from monitoring weIls are pIaced into
laboratory prepared containers, seaIed with tight fitting caps, labeIed, and
stored in a cooIed ice chest whiIe awaiting deIivery to AgricuIture & Priority
PoIlutants Laboratories (APPL), a CaIifornia-certified Environmental
Laboratory Accreditation Program (ELAP) laboratory in CIovis, CaIifornia.
The sampIes are anaIyzed for EC, nitrate as nitrogen (NOs-N), and
ammonium as nitrogen (NH,-N).
B. Groundwater EIevation Map
A Groundwater EIevation Map, based on avaiIabIe information, was prepared
for the March 08 and September 06, 2023, sampIing events. WeIl locations,
depth to groundwater, and groundwater eIevations for the events, as
appIicabIe, are iIlustrated in Appendix A Figure 1.
